Functional steps to implement use case SR.BOD.CLIENT.RTProvision.RouteConstraint.Reuse.OTN_001:1. Validate the entered route constraint.2. Identify the existing OTN circuit to be reused.3. Check the availability status of the identified OTN circuit.4. If the identified OTN circuit is available, proceed to the next step.5. Check if the identified OTN circuit meets the required route constraint criteria.6. If the identified OTN circuit meets the criteria, proceed to the next step.7. Generate a new RT Provision request for reusing the identified OTN circuit.8. Update the relevant attributes and parameters for the reused OTN circuit.9. Validate the updated attributes and parameters.10. Submit the RT Provision request for reusing the OTN circuit.11. Verify the status of the RT Provision request.12. If the OTN circuit reuse is successful, notify the user about the successful reuse.13. If the OTN circuit reuse is unsuccessful, notify the user about the failure.14. End the use case.
